# <a name="office-365-management-activity-api-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-103">Office 365 管理活动 API 架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-103">Office 365 Management Activity API schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-104">Office 365 管理活动 API 架构作为两层数据服务提供：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-104">The Office 365 Management Activity API schema is provided as a data service in  two layers:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-105">**常见架构**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-105">**Common schema**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-106">用于访问核心 Office 365 审核概念（如 Record Type、Creation Time、User Type 和 Action），以及提供核心维度（如 User ID）、具体位置细节（如 Client IP address）和特定于产品的属性（如 Object ID）的接口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-106">The interface to access core Office 365 auditing concepts such as Record Type, Creation Time, User Type, and Action as well as to provide core dimensions (such as User ID), location specifics (such as Client IP address), and product-specific properties (such as Object ID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-107">它建立一致且统一的视图，以便用户使用适当参数在少数顶级视图中提取所有 Office 365 审核数据，并为所有数据源提供固定架构，从而极大地降低了学习成本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-107">It establishes consistent and uniform views for users to extract all Office 365 audit data in a few top level views with the appropriate parameters, and provides a fixed schema for all the data sources, which significantly reduces the cost of learning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-108">常见架构源自于归每个产品团队（如 Exchange、SharePoint、Azure Active Directory、Yammer 和 OneDrive for Business）所有的产品数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-108">Common schema is sourced from product data that is owned by each product team, such as Exchange, SharePoint, Azure Active Directory, Yammer, and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-109">Object ID 字段可由产品团队扩展，添加特定于产品的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-109">The Object ID field can be extended by product teams to add product specific properties.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-110">**特定于产品的架构**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-110">**Product-specific schema**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-111">基于常见架构，提供一组特定于产品的属性；例如，Sway 架构、SharePoint 架构、OneDrive for Business 架构以及 Exchange 管理员架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-111">Built on top of the Common schema to provide a set of product-specific attributes; for example, Sway schema, SharePoint schema, OneDrive for Business schema, and Exchange admin schema.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-112">**对于你自身的情况应使用哪个层？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-112">**Which layer should you use for your scenario?**</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="fda95-113">一般情况下，如果数据在较高层中可用，则不要回到较低层。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-113">In general, if the data is available in a higher layer, don't go back to a lower layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-114">换言之，如果可在特定于产品的架构中满足数据要求，则不需要返回到常见架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-114">In other words, if the data requirement can be fit in a product-specific schema, you don't need to go back to the Common schema.</span></span> 

## <a name="office-365-management-api-schemas"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-115">Office 365 管理 API 架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-115">Office 365 Management API schemas</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-116">本文详细介绍了常见架构以及每个特定于产品的架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-116">This article provides details on the Common schema as well as each of the product specific schemas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-117">下表描述了可用的架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-117">The following table describes the available schemas.</span></span> 

|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-118">架构名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-118">Name of schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-119">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-119">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|
|[<span data-ttu-id="fda95-120">常见架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-120">Common schema</span></span>](#common-schema)|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-121">用于提取 Record Type、User ID、Client IP、User Type 和 Action 以及核心维度，如用户属性（如 UserID）、位置属性（如 Client IP）和特定于产品的属性（如 Object ID）的视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-121">The view to extract Record Type, User ID, Client IP, User type and Action along with core dimensions such as user properties (such as UserID), location properties (such as Client IP), and product-specific properties (such as Object Id).</span></span>|
|[<span data-ttu-id="fda95-122">SharePoint 基本架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-122">SharePoint Base schema</span></span>](#sharepoint-base-schema)|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-123">使用特定于所有 SharePoint 审核数据的属性扩展常见架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-123">Extends the Common schema with the properties specific to all SharePoint audit data.</span></span>|

## <a name="common-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-172">常见架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-172">Common schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-173">**EntityType 名称**：AuditRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-173">**EntityType Name**: AuditRecord</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-174">参数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-174">Parameter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-175">类型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-175">Type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-176">强制？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-176">Mandatory?</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-177">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-177">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-178">Id</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-178">Id</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-179">Combination GUIDEdm.Guid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-179">Combination GUIDEdm.Guid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-180">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-180">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-181">审核记录的唯一标识符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-181">Unique identifier of an audit record.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-182">RecordType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-182">RecordType</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-183">Self.[AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-183">Self.[AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-184">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-184">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-185">记录指示的操作类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-185">The type of operation indicated by the record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-186">有关审核日志记录类型的详细信息表，请参阅 [AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-186">See the [AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype) table for details on the types of audit log records.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-187">CreationTime</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-187">CreationTime</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-188">Edm.Date</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-188">Edm.Date</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-189">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-189">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-190">用户执行活动时的协调世界时 (UTC) 日期和时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-190">The date and time in Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) when the user performed the activity.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-191">Operation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-191">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-192">Edm.String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-192">Edm.String</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-193">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-193">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-194">用户或管理员活动的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-194">The name of the user or admin activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-195">有关最常见操作/活动的说明，请参阅[在 Office 365 保护中心搜索审核日志](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=708432)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-195">For a description of the most common operations/activities, see [Search the audit log in the Office 365 Protection Center](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=708432).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-196">对于 Exchange 管理员活动，此属性标识已运行的 cmdlet 名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-196">For Exchange admin activity, this property identifies the name of the cmdlet that was run.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-197">对于 DLp 事件，这可以是“DLP 架构”下描述的“DlpRuleMatch”、“DlpRuleUndo”或“DlpInfo”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-197">For Dlp events, this can be "DlpRuleMatch", "DlpRuleUndo" or "DlpInfo", which are described under "DLP schema" below.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-218">ResultStatus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-218">ResultStatus</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-219">Edm.String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-219">Edm.String</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-220">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-220">No</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-221">指示操作（在 Operation 属性中指定）成功还是失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-221">Indicates whether the action (specified in the Operation property) was successful or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-222">可能的值为：**Succeeded**、**PartiallySucceeded** 或 **Failed**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-222">Possible values are **Succeeded**, **PartiallySucceeded**, or **Failed**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-223">对于 Exchange 管理员活动，值为 **True** 或 **False**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-223">For Exchange admin activity, the value is either **True** or **False**.</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="fda95-224">**重要说明**：不同的工作负载可能会覆盖 ResultStatus 属性的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-224">**Important**: Different workloads may overwrite the value of the ResultStatus property.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-225">例如，对于 Azure Active Directory STS 登录事件，ResultStatus 的“**已成功**”值仅指示 HTTP 操作成功；这并不意味着登录成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-225">For example, for Azure Active Directory STS logon events, a value of **Succeeded** for ResultStatus indicates only that the HTTP operation was successful; it doesn't mean the logon was successful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-226">若要确定实际登录是否成功，请参阅 [Azure Active Directory STS 登录架构](#azure-active-directory-secure-token-service-sts-logon-schema)中的 LogonError 属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-226">To determine if the actual logon was successful or not, see the LogonError property in the [Azure Active Directory STS Logon schema](#azure-active-directory-secure-token-service-sts-logon-schema).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-227">如果登录失败，则此属性的值将包含登录尝试失败的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-227">If the logon failed, the value of this property will contain the reason for the failed logon attempt.</span></span> |

|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-233">UserID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-233">UserId</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-234">Edm.string</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-234">Edm.string</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-235">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-235">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-236">执行导致记录被记录的操作（在 Operation 属性中指定）的用户的 UPN（用户主体名称）；例如 `my_name@my_domain_name`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-236">The UPN (User Principal Name) of the user who performed the action (specified in the Operation property) that resulted in the record being logged; for example, `my_name@my_domain_name`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-237">注意，系统帐户执行的活动记录（例如 SHAREPOINT\system 或 NT AUTHORITY\SYSTEM）也包括在内。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-237">Note that records for activity performed by system accounts (such as SHAREPOINT\system or NT AUTHORITY\SYSTEM) are also included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-238">在 SharePoint 中，UserId 属性中的另一个数值显示为 app@sharepoint。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-238">In SharePoint, another value display in the UserId property is app@sharepoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-239">这表明执行活动的“用户”是在 SharePoint 中拥有必要权限的应用程序，代表用户、管理员或服务执行组织范围内操作（例如，搜索 SharePoint 网站或 OneDrive 帐户）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-239">This indicates that the "user" who performed the activity was an application that has the necessary permissions in SharePoint to perform organization-wide actions (such as search a SharePoint site or OneDrive account) on behalf of a user, admin, or service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-240">有关详细信息，请参阅[审核记录中的 app@sharepoint 用户](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/compliance/search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-240">For more information, see [The app@sharepoint user in audit records](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/compliance/search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-241">ClientIP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-241">ClientIP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-242">Edm.String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-242">Edm.String</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-243">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-243">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="fda95-244">记录活动时使用的设备的 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-244">The IP address of the device that was used when the activity was logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-245">IP 地址显示为 IPv4 或 IPv6 地址格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-245">The IP address is displayed in either an IPv4 or IPv6 address format.</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="fda95-246">对于某些服务，此属性中显示的值可能是代表用户调用服务的受信任应用程序（例如，Web 应用上的 Office）的 IP 地址，而不是执行活动的人员使用的设备的 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-246">For some services, the value displayed in this property might be the IP address for a trusted application (for example, Office on the web apps) calling into the service on behalf of a user and not the IP address of the device used by person who performed the activity.</span></span> <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="fda95-247">此外，对于与 Azure Active Directory 相关的事件，不会记录 IP 地址，并且 ClientIP 属性的值为 `null`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-247">Also, for Azure Active Directory-related events, the IP address isn't logged and the value for the ClientIP property is `null`.</span></span>|

## <a name="sharepoint-file-operations"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-861">SharePoint 文件操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-861">SharePoint file operations</span></span>

)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-913">For information about the SharePoint Sharing schema, see [Use sharing auditing in the Office 365 audit log](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/compliance/use-sharing-auditing

## <a name="dlp-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-1562">DLP 架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1562">DLP schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-1563">DLP 事件可用于 Exchange Online、SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive For Business。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1563">DLP events are available for Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, and OneDrive For Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1564">请注意，Exchange 中的 DLP 事件仅适用于基于统一 DLP 策略的事件（例如通过安全与合规中心配置的事件）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1564">Note that DLP events in Exchange are only available for events based on unified DLP policy (e.g. configured via Security & Compliance Center).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1565">不支持基于 Exchange 传输规则的 DLP 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1565">DLP events based on Exchange Transport Rules are not supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-1566">在常见架构中，DLP（数据丢失防护）事件始终具有 UserKey=“DlpAgent”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1566">DLP (Data Loss Prevention) events will always have UserKey="DlpAgent" in the common schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1567">有三种类型的 DlpEvents，它们被存储为常见架构的 Operation 属性值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1567">There are three types of DlpEvents that are stored as the value of the Operation property of the common schema:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1568">DlpRuleMatch：表示匹配某个规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1568">DlpRuleMatch - This indicates a rule was matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1569">Exchange 和 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中存在这些事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1569">These events exist in both Exchange and SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1570">对于 Exchange，它包含误报和重写信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1570">For Exchange it includes false positive and override information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1571">对于 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business，误报和重写会生成单独事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1571">For SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, false positive and overrides generate separate events.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1572">DlpRuleUndo：仅存在于 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中，指示以前应用的策略操作已“撤销”，因为用户指定误报/重写，或者因为文件不再受策略的制约（由于策略更改或文档内容的更改）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1572">DlpRuleUndo - These only exist in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, and indicate a previously applied policy action has been "undone" – either because of false positive/override designation by user, or because the document is no longer subject to policy (either due to policy change or change to content in doc).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1573">DlpInfo：仅存在于 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中，指示指定的误报，但没有“撤销”任何操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1573">DlpInfo - These only exist in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business and indicate a false positive designation but no action was "undone."</span></span>

### <a name="sharepointmetadata-complex-type"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-1599">SharePointMetadata 复杂类型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1599">SharePointMetadata complex type</span></span>

## <a name="security-and-compliance-alerts-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-1851">安全与合规警报架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1851">Security and Compliance Alerts schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-1852">警报信号包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1852">Alert signals include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1853">基于[安全与合规中心的警报策略](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/alert-policies#default-alert-policies)生成的所有警报。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1853">All alerts generated based on [Alert policies in Security & Compliance Center](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/alert-policies#default-alert-policies).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1854">在 [Office 365 云应用安全](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-cas-overview)和 [Microsoft Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/cloud-app-security/what-is-cloud-app-security) 中生成的 Office 365 相关警报。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1854">Office 365 related alerts generated in [Office 365 Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-cas-overview) and [Microsoft Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/cloud-app-security/what-is-cloud-app-security).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-1855">这些事件的 UserId 和 UserKey 始终为 SecurityComplianceAlerts。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1855">The UserId and UserKey of these events are always SecurityComplianceAlerts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1856">有两种类型的警报信号，它们被存储为常见架构的 Operation 属性值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1856">There are two types of alert signals which are stored as the value of the Operation property of the common schema:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1857">AlertTriggered：由于策略匹配而生成新警报。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1857">AlertTriggered - A new alert is generated due to a policy match.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1858">AlertEntityGenerated：向警报添加新实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1858">AlertEntityGenerated - A new entity is added to an alert.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1859">此事件仅适用于基于 Office 365 安全与合规中心的警报策略生成的警报。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1859">This event is only applicable to alerts generated based on Alert policies in the Office 365 Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1860">每个生成的警报都可与一个或多个上述事件相关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1860">Each generated alert can be associated with one or multiple of these events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1861">例如，如果任何用户在 5 分钟内删除了超过 100 个文件，则定义警报策略以触发警报。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1861">For example, an alert policy is defined to trigger an alert if any user deletes more than 100 files in 5 minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-1862">如果两个用户几乎同时超过阈值，则会有两个 AlertEntityGenerated 事件，但只有一个 AlertTriggered 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-1862">If two users exceed the threshold around the same time, there will be two AlertEntityGenerated events, but only one AlertTriggered event.</span></span>

## <a name="office-365-advanced-threat-protection-and-threat-investigation-and-response-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-2333">Office 365 高级威胁防护与威胁调查和响应架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2333">Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Investigation and Response schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-2334">[Office 365 高级威胁防护](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-atp) (ATP) 与威胁调查和响应事件适用于具有 Office 365 高级威胁防护计划 1、Office 365 高级威胁防护计划 2 或 E5 订阅的 Office 365 客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2334">[Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-atp) (ATP) and Threat Investigation and Response events are available for Office 365 customers who have an Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 1, Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 2, or an E5 subscription.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2335">Office 365 ATP 源中的每个事件对应以下确定为包含威胁的事件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2335">Each event in the Office 365 ATP feed corresponds to the following that were determined to contain a threat:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2336">由组织中的用户发送或接收电子邮件，同时对送达的邮件进行检测，并从[零时差自动清除](https://support.office.com/article/Zero-hour-auto-purge-protection-against-spam-and-malware-96deb75f-64e8-4c10-b570-84c99c674e15)检测邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2336">An email message sent by or received by a user in the organization with detections that are made on messages at delivery time and from [Zero hour auto purge](https://support.office.com/article/Zero-hour-auto-purge-protection-against-spam-and-malware-96deb75f-64e8-4c10-b570-84c99c674e15).</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2337">组织中的用户单击 URL，基于 [Office 365 ATP 安全链接](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-safe-links)保护被检测为恶意。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2337">URLs clicked by a user in the organization that were detected as malicious at time-of-click based on [Office 365 ATP Safe Links](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-safe-links) protection.</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2338">SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business 或 Microsoft Teams 中由 [Office 365 ATP](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-for-spo-odb-and-teams) 保护检测为“恶意”的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2338">A file within SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Microsoft Teams that was detected as malicious by [Office 365 ATP](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-for-spo-odb-and-teams) protection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2339">触发并启动[自动调查](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office)的警报。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2339">An alert that is triggered and that started an [automated investigation](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2340">Office 365 高级威胁防护与 Office 365 威胁调查和响应（先前称为 Office 365 威胁智能）功能现在是 Office 365 高级威胁防护计划 2 的一部分，具有其他威胁防护功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2340">Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection and Office 365 Threat Investigation and Response (formerly known as Office 365 Threat Intelligence) capabilites are now part of Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 2, with additional threat protection capabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2341">若要了解详细信息，请参阅 [Office 365 ATP 计划和定价](https://products.office.com/exchange/advance-threat-protection)与 [Office 365 ATP 服务说明](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-advanced-threat-protection-service-description)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2341">To learn more, see [Office 365 ATP plans and pricing](https://products.office.com/exchange/advance-threat-protection) and the [Office 365 ATP Service Description](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-advanced-threat-protection-service-description).</span></span>

## <a name="automated-investigation-and-response-events-in-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="fda95-2668">Office 365 中的自动调查和响应事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2668">Automated investigation and response events in Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-2669">[Office 365 自动调查和响应 (AIR)](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office) 事件适用于其订阅中包含 Office 365 高级威胁防护计划 2 或 Office 365 E5 的 Office 365 客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2669">[Office 365 automated investigation and response (AIR)](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office) events are available for Office 365 customers who have a subscription that includes Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 2 or Office 365 E5.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2670">将根据调查状态的变化记录调查事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2670">Investigation events are logged based on a change in investigation status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2671">例如，当管理员执行将调查状态从“挂起的操作”更改为“已完成”的操作时，将记录一个事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2671">For example, when an administrator takes an action that changes the status of an investigation from Pending Actions to Completed, an event is logged.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="fda95-2672">目前，仅记录自动调查事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2672">Currently, only automated investigation are logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2673">（手动生成调查的事件即将提供。）将记录以下状态值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2673">(Events for manually generated investigations are coming soon.) The following status values are logged:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2674">已开始调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2674">Investigation Started</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2675">未发现威胁</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2675">No threats found</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2676">已由系统终止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2676">Terminated by System</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2677">挂起的操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2677">Pending Action</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2678">发现威胁</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2678">Threats Found</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2679">已修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2679">Remediated</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2680">已失败</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2680">Failed</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2681">已通过限制终止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2681">Terminated by throttling</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2682">已由用户终止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2682">Terminated By User</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="fda95-2683">正在运行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fda95-2683">Running</span></span>
